***ansichtkaart.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ansichtkaart.html>ansichtkaart</a> (21714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Partially adapted borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ansichtskarte</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ansichtkaart.html>ansichtkaart</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ansichtkaarten.html>ansichtkaarten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ansichtkaart.html>ansichtkaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A picture postcard.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ansicht</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:postkaart.html>postkaart</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">prentbriefkaart</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zichtkaart</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ansichtkaart.html>ansichtkaart</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

***antenne.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:antenne.html>antenne</a> (11593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:antenne.html>antenne</a></i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">antenna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">antenna</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:antenne.html>antenne</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:antennes.html>antennes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">antennen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:antenne.html>antennetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>antenna (feeler organ on the head of an insect)</li>
<li>antenna (device to receive or transmit radio signals)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***anticlimax.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:anticlimax.html>anticlimax</a> (45904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">anti-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">climax</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:anticlimax.html>anticlimax</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">anticlimaxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A failed or reverse climax, <i>particularly</i>:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">narratology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unsatisfying resolution to a narrative, usually owing to a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:machina.html>machina</a></i> or similarly trivial resolution of the main conflict.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rhetoric</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An abrupt descent (either deliberate or unintentional) from the dignity of the idea which the speaker or writer appeared to be aiming for.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">partial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bathos</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">anticlimactic</span></li></ul>

***antwoorden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:antwoorden.html>antwoorden</a> (1596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">antworden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">antworden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*andawurdijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:antwoorden.html>antwoorden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to answer, reply
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geantwoord.html>geantwoord</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not <b>answered</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***apenkooi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:apenkooi.html>apenkooi</a> (77354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ape”, “monkey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kooi.html>kooi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:apenkooi.html>apenkooi</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:apenkooi.html>apenkooien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:apenkooi.html>apenkooitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A place where <a href = vnd.unilang:apes.html>apes</a> and/or <a href = vnd.unilang:monkeys.html>monkeys</a> are kept, an apery.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> games<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A variation of tag, usually played in school <a href = vnd.unilang:gyms.html>gyms</a>, where players are not allowed to touch the floor and can only move about <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mats.html>mats</a>, vaulting <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bars.html>bars</a>, ropes, etc. Anyone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> caught or touches the floor <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to leave the field of play.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">apocalypticus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀποκαλυπτικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apokaluptikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
